** Avoidance during activity (R Areas and Class A) **
AC A
SP 0,2,255,0,0
SB -1,-1,-1
V X=51:30:00 N 3:00:00 E
DC 0.05

** Clearance requested (Class C and D) **
AC C
SP 0,2,0,0,255
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

AC D
SP 0,2,0,0,255
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

** No Clearance requested when VMC (Class E) **
AC E
SP 0,2,200,200,255
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

** Comply with Restrictions (Restricted Areas)
AC R
SP 0,2,0,0,0
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

** Danger Areas **
AC Q
SP 0,1,255,0,0
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

** Permanent Avoidance (Prohibited or Restricted Areas) **
AC P
SP 0,1,255,0,0
SB 255,0,0
DC 0.05

** Dispensatory Glider Activity **
AC W
SP 0,2,0,255,0
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05

** Natural Parcs and Reserves, Parachute Activity **
AC GP
SP 1,1,255,0,0
SB -1,-1,-1
DC 0.05
